Raajaneeti dandana cheta tappa maroka vidhangaa nirvartinchabada ledu. Kanuka neevu sokhamunu vadili goppagoppa yaagamulu, yagnamulu chesi chakkagaa raajyaanni paalimchu. Dharmanandanaa ! Nee tammulu nee bhaarya neemaata manninchi pannemdella aranyavaasam oka edu agnaatavaasam chesi kashtamulu anubhavinchaaru. ippudu neevu vaari maata manninchi vaariki sukhasaamtulu kalugacheyyi. Viraagi ayi adavulaku velli devatalaku pitrdevatalaku baadha kaliginchaku. Neeku nyaayasaasastram baagaa telusu. Prajala manobhishtam telusukuni sishtarakshana, dushtasikshana chesi dandaneetini amalu parache raajuku annee subhaale kalugutaayi. Prajala aadaayam nundi aarava bhaagam pannugaavasoolu cheyyi. Prajalanmu kannalabiddala vale paalimchu. Ide mokshamuku maargam chooputundi. Nee manasulo vunna bhayam samsayam vadili pettu. kaani dharmaraajaa raaju ahankarinchi kaama krodhavasudai prajaakantakangaa paaliste atadiki prajalu chese paapamlo naalgavabhaagam labhistundi. satruvulanu nirmoolinchadam kshatriya dharmam, paapaatmulaina raajulato sandhi chesukovadam dosham, satruvulato sandhi chesukuni tana raajyamlo konta bhaagam ivvadam manchidikaadu. yuddham chesi raajyarakshana cheyadam kshatriya dharmamam. kanuka neevu yuddham chesinanduku chimtimpa pani ledu. duryodhanudito sandhi chesukoka povadam valana ee ghora yuddham sambhavinchindi anukovadam nee avivekam poorvam hayagreevudane raaju yuddhamulu chesi satruvulanu jayinchi, dundagulanu sikshinchi. sanmaargulanu rakshinchi, yagnayaagaadulu chesi, pragaaranjakangaa paalinchi tudaku sadgati pondaadu. kanuka yuddhamulu raajulaku keedu cheyyavu. yuddhamlo chaavadam, champadam sahajam kanuka neevu anumaanam vadili samardhulaina raajodyogulanu niyaminchi raajyakaaryamulu nirvahinchumu " annaadu.
